And when the dislocation is in front, it is necessary to extend the sick leg quickly, and according to what I have said; and put your hands on the sore angle, then press with the other hand, and extend it downwards towards the knee. 
Et se li dislocations est au defuer, si ne covient pas estendre le malaide aval, ne lever sus la terre, ains covient qu’il soit ausi com se li hainche estoit desaluee au defuer, si com nos avons dit dou couchement sus les II hainches; et soit sus sa faice, et li lien estendut si com nos avons dit ci devant, et doit om presser sus la jointure a la table; et sera a point quant li malaides estendra ses jambes, et elles seront igalz; adonques ajoste les cuixes, et met l’emplaustre, et l’estrain d’un bendeil, si que li hainche ne se mueve; et se repose III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie, et met l’emplaustre sus; et se tu vois qu’elles soient igalz, si l’estrain, si com devant, et le laisse III jors; puis le deslie, et lou fai aler belement, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And if the dislocation is in the shoulder, it is not fitting to extend the patient downwards, nor raise him up on the ground, but he should be as if his shoulder were dislocated upwards, as we have said about lying on both hips; and he should be on his face, and the bandage extended as we have said before, and one must press on the joint at the table; and it will be set when the patient extends his legs, and they will be equal; then adjust the thighs, and apply the plaster, and bind him with a bandage so that the shoulder does not move; and he rests for three days or four, then unbind him, and apply the plaster on top; and if you see that they are equal, bind him as before, and leave him for three days; then unbind him, and let him walk well, as long as the limb is comfortable. 
de la dislocation dou genoil	Of knee dislocation 
Li genous est desaluez selonc III manieres: c’est a savoir, dedens et defuer, et derrier; et ne desalue point devant.	The knee is dislocated according to three manners: that is to say, inward and outward, and behind; and it does not dislocate forward. 
Et li signes si est que tu comande au malaide qu’il plie sa jambe a sa cuixe, et s’ele ne s’aert a sa cuixe, saiches qu’il est desaluez; et li restauration de toutes si est que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et estende sa jambe s’il puet, et li met ton dos sus sa faice, et met son piet sus tes piez; puis pren son genoil a tes paumes, et retrai entre tes dois, puis plie les II costez dou genoil forment; et uns autres ministres estende son piet, tant que li genous reviegne a son leu, et li signes est qu’il aert bien sa jambe a sa cuixe legierement; et met l’emplastre sus, et fai aerdre la jambe a la cuixe, et les loie ensamble fort III jors ou IIII, puis le deslie; et ne se travaille mie li malaides d’aler, tant que li membres soit confortez.	And the signs are such that you command the patient to bend his leg at his thigh, and if it does not bend at his thigh, know that it is dislocated; and the restoration of all such is that you make the patient sit upright, and extend his leg if he can, and put your back on his face, and put his foot on your feet; then take his knee in your palms, and draw between your thighs, then bend the two sides where the knee forms; and another minister extends his foot, as long as the knee returns to its place, and the sign is that he bends his leg at his thigh lightly; and put the plaster on it, and make the leg air at the thigh, and bind them together tightly for three days or four, then untie it; and let the patient not bother to walk, as long as the limb is strengthened. 
Et se li membres n’est a point, si aministre estendement fort, si com nos avons dit en la cure de la hainche, tant qu’il soit sanez	And if the limb is not set, administer strong extension, as we have said in the treatment of the hip, until it is healed 
de la dislocation dou talon	Of the dislocation of the heel 
Li talons est aucune fois esmeus, et aucune fois desaluez plenement, et dedens et defuer.	The talon is sometimes loosened, and sometimes completely dislocated, within and without. 
Et li signes si est que li cheville est enflee, et tent avant a la partie ou elle est desaluee: li ramenemens si est legier, et le doit on estendre legierement a ses mains quant il est esmeus soulement.	And the signs are that the ankle is swollen and tense before the part where it is dislocated; the resetting should be gentle, and one must gently stretch the limb with his hands when he is only relaxed. 
Et quant il est desaluez dou tot, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide droit, et le tigne I ministres fors par la jambe, desus la cheville; puis trai le piet a toi a ta main destre, et puis a la senestre II fois, puis l’estent en haut, et boute bellement lou piet en haut; et fai ce II fois, si com nos avons dit, em boutant et en traiant lou piet; s’elle revient, c’est bien; se ce non, si rencomence l’ovraige, car il revient; et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche I passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide; puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a I liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet; puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent; puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	And when it is dislocated altogether, it is fitting that you make the patient sit upright, and hold them firmly by the leg, above the ankle; then draw the foot towards you with your right hand, and then to the left twice, then stretch it upwards, and push the foot up nicely; and do this twice, as we have said, by pushing and pulling the foot; if it returns, it is well; if not, start the work again, for it will return; and if it cannot return thus, make the patient lie on their back on the ground, and fix a strong pole firmly in the ground between their thighs, and tie cloths around, so that they do not hurt the patient; then have one minister hold the thigh, and another minister extend the foot with their hands or with a rope which they tie above the ankle of the foot; then each minister stretches equally, and the pole is now placed between the patient's thighs to hold the patient when it is stretched; then place the ministers' hands equal to the dislocation, and have another minister hold the healthy leg below, and the dislocation will return quickly. 
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois; puis le laisse II jors ou III, et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par IIII jors; et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And when it is firm, apply the plaster and bandages on top, and hold them in place, and bind the foot to the leg, and protect the nerves which are above the ankle behind so that the bandages are not too tight; then leave it for II days or III, and if the bandages loosen, tighten them; then unbind it on the third day or the fourth, and forbid the patient from walking for IV days; and if he walks before this time, it is not certain that it will not dislocate again. 
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if an abscess comes, it is necessary that you soothe it, as we have said elsewhere, until it is healed. 
des dois	of two
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the two are dislocated, if they fit together well, extend them without effort, and this is a light matter. 
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus I leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne; et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a II chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse III jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if the dislocation is in any joint of the back or foot, it is fitting that you make the patient sit on a flat place or on a table straight and put your foot on what appears of those joints, then press with your foot strongly, until it returns; and when it is even and nothing appears, put under the sole of the foot a table with two legs, then strain it strongly, and leave it for three days, then untie it; and let him rest, until he is healed. 
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	of wound and of dislocation together 
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert: si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis; et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit; et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne; et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis; et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples; et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors.	When a wound comes with the dislocation and one wishes to restore it, many times it happens that the patient dies: so do not be presumptuous in the cure if you are not wise in the art and have not used it for a long time, and if you are not pitiful and merciful and slow, do not dare; and use at the beginning soothing things, hot poultices, and leave the patient in God's hand if you do not see hope of health.
Amen	Amen
